<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Parlamento_do_Mercosul_2010_Mercosul_(4999372816).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Parlamento_do_Mercosul_2010_Mercosul_%284999372816%29.jpg/220px-Parlamento_do_Mercosul_2010_Mercosul_%284999372816%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Parlamento_do_Mercosul_2010_Mercosul_%284999372816%29.jpg/330px-Parlamento_do_Mercosul_2010_Mercosul_%284999372816%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Parlamento_do_Mercosul_2010_Mercosul_%284999372816%29.jpg/440px-Parlamento_do_Mercosul_2010_Mercosul_%284999372816%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4288" data-file-height="2848" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Parlamento_do_Mercosul_2010_Mercosul_(4999372816).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Mercosur_Parliament" title="Mercosur Parliament">Mercosur Parliament</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Asunci%C3%B3n" title="Treaty of Asunción">Asunción Treaty</a> and <a href="/wiki/Protocol_of_Ouro_Preto" title="Protocol of Ouro Preto">Ouro Preto Protocol</a> established the basis for the institutional Mercosur structure, creating the <a href="/wiki/Common_Market" class="mw-redirect" title="Common Market">Common Market</a> Council and the Common Market Group, both of which function at the outset of the transition phase. As provided for in this Treaty, before establishing the common market the member nations must call a special meeting to determine the definitive institutional structure for the public agencies managing Mercosur, as well as define the specific functions of each agency and the decision making process.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Common_Market_Council">Common Market Council</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Common Market Council">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Council is the highest-level agency of Mercosur with the authority to conduct its policy, and responsibility for compliance with the objects and time frames set forth in the Asuncion Treaty. The Council is composed of the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs" title="Ministry of Foreign Affairs">Ministers of Foreign Affairs</a> and the Economy (or the equivalent) of all five countries. Member states preside over the Council in rotating alphabetical order, for six-month periods. Meetings: Council members shall meet whenever necessary, but at least once a year. The presidents of the member nations shall partake of the annual Common Market Council meeting whenever possible. Decision Making: Council decisions shall be made by consensus, with representation of all member states.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Common_Market_Group">Common Market Group</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Common Market Group">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:XXX_Cumbre_del_Mercosur_-_C%C3%B3rdoba_-_21JUL06_-_presidenciagovar.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/XXX_Cumbre_del_Mercosur_-_C%C3%B3rdoba_-_21JUL06_-_presidenciagovar.jpg/220px-XXX_Cumbre_del_Mercosur_-_C%C3%B3rdoba_-_21JUL06_-_presidenciagovar.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/XXX_Cumbre_del_Mercosur_-_C%C3%B3rdoba_-_21JUL06_-_presidenciagovar.jpg/330px-XXX_Cumbre_del_Mercosur_-_C%C3%B3rdoba_-_21JUL06_-_presidenciagovar.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/XXX_Cumbre_del_Mercosur_-_C%C3%B3rdoba_-_21JUL06_-_presidenciagovar.jpg/440px-XXX_Cumbre_del_Mercosur_-_C%C3%B3rdoba_-_21JUL06_-_presidenciagovar.jpg 2x" data-file-width="449" data-file-height="298" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:XXX_Cumbre_del_Mercosur_-_C%C3%B3rdoba_-_21JUL06_-_presidenciagovar.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mercosur reunion in <a href="/wiki/C%C3%B3rdoba,_Argentina" title="Córdoba, Argentina">Cordoba</a>, 2006.</div></div></div>
<p>The Group is the executive body of Mercosur, and is coordinated by the Ministries of Foreign Affairs of the member states. Its basic duties are to cause compliance with the Asuncion Treaty and to take resolutions required for implementation of the decisions made by the Council. Furthermore, it can initiate practical measures for trade opening, coordination of <a href="/wiki/Macroeconomic" class="mw-redirect" title="Macroeconomic">macroeconomic</a> policies, and negotiation of agreements with nonmember states and international agencies, participating when need be in resolution of controversies under Mercosur. It has the authority to organize, coordinate and supervise Work Subgroups and to call special meetings to deal with issues of interest. Composition: The Common Market Group shall be made up of four permanent members and four alternates from each member state, representing the following <a href="/wiki/Public" title="Public">public</a> <a href="/wiki/Government_agency" title="Government agency">agencies</a>: (i) the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs" title="Ministry of Foreign Affairs">Ministry of Foreign Affairs</a>; (ii) the <a href="/wiki/Finance_minister" title="Finance minister">Ministry of Economy</a>, or the equivalent (from industry, foreign affairs and/or economic coordination); and (iii) the <a href="/wiki/Central_Bank" class="mw-redirect" title="Central Bank">Central Bank</a>. The members of the Common Market Group appointed by a given member state will constitute the National Section of the Common Market Group for that particular nation. Meetings: The Common Market Group will meet ordinarily at least once every quarter in the member states, in rotating alphabetical order. Special meetings may be freely called at any time, at any previously scheduled place. The meetings will be coordinated by the Head of the Delegation of the host member state. Decision Making: Common Market Group decisions shall be made by consensus, with the representation of all member states. The official Mercosur languages will be Portuguese and Spanish, and the official version of all work papers will be prepared in the language of the country hosting the meeting.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:194px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mercosul-Bandeira.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/67/Mercosul-Bandeira.jpg" decoding="async" width="192" height="320" class="thumbimage" data-file-width="192" data-file-height="320" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mercosul-Bandeira.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mercosur/Mercosul's flag in the city of <a href="/wiki/Bras%C3%ADlia" title="Brasília">Brasília</a>, Brazil.</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Administrative_and_socioeconomic">Administrative and socioeconomic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Administrative and socioeconomic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Administrative Office will keep documents and issue the Mercosur official bulletin in both Portuguese and Spanish, and will also be charged with communicating the activities of the Common Market Group so as to allow for the maximum disclosure of decisions and the relevant documentation. The <a href="/wiki/Socioeconomic" class="mw-redirect" title="Socioeconomic">Socioeconomic</a> Advisory Forum is consultative by nature, and represents the various socioeconomic sectors of the member nations.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Work_subgroups">Work subgroups</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Work subgroups">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Directly subordinated to the <a href="/wiki/Common_Market" class="mw-redirect" title="Common Market">Common Market</a> Group, the Work Subgroups draw up the minutes of the decisions to submit for the consideration of the Council, and conduct studies on specific Mercosur concerns. The work subgroups are the following: commercial matters; customs matters; technical standards; tax and monetary policies relating to trade; land transport; sea transport; industrial and technology policies; agricultural policy; energy policy; coordination of macroeconomic policies; and labor, employment and social security matters. meetings. The meetings of the Work subgroups will be held quarterly, alternating in every member state, in alphabetical order, or at the Common Market Group Administrative Office. Activities will be carried out by the Work Subgroups in two stages: preparatory and conclusive. In the preparatory stage, the members of the Work Subgroups may request the participation of representatives from the private sector of each member state. The decision-making stage is reserved exclusively for official representatives of the member states. The delegations of representatives from the private sector in the preparatory stage of the Work Subgroup activities will have a maximum of three representatives for each member state directly involved in any of the stages of the production, distribution or consumption process for the products that fall within the scope of the subgroup's activities.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Joint_Parliamentary_Committee">Joint Parliamentary Committee</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Joint Parliamentary Committee">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:17072019_C%C3%BApula_de_Chefes_de_Estado_do_Mercosul.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/17072019_C%C3%BApula_de_Chefes_de_Estado_do_Mercosul.jpg/220px-17072019_C%C3%BApula_de_Chefes_de_Estado_do_Mercosul.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/17072019_C%C3%BApula_de_Chefes_de_Estado_do_Mercosul.jpg/330px-17072019_C%C3%BApula_de_Chefes_de_Estado_do_Mercosul.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/17072019_C%C3%BApula_de_Chefes_de_Estado_do_Mercosul.jpg/440px-17072019_C%C3%BApula_de_Chefes_de_Estado_do_Mercosul.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3506" data-file-height="1978" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:17072019_C%C3%BApula_de_Chefes_de_Estado_do_Mercosul.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Presidents of Mercosur at 2019 summit, <a href="/wiki/Santa_Fe,_Argentina" title="Santa Fe, Argentina">Santa Fe</a>, Argentina.</div></div></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Committee" title="Committee">Committee</a> will have both an advisory and decision-making nature; with powers to submit proposals as well. It will be competent, inter alia, to: follow up on the <a href="/wiki/Regional_integration" title="Regional integration">integration</a> process and keep the respective <a href="/wiki/Congress" title="Congress">Congresses</a> informed; Take the necessary steps for the future instatement of a <a href="/wiki/Mercosur_Parliament" title="Mercosur Parliament">Mercosur Parliament</a>; Organize subcommittees to examine matters relating to the integration process; Submit its recommendations to the Common Market Council and Group as to how the integration process should be conducted and Southern Common Market formed; Make the adjustments necessary to harmonize the laws of the different member states and submit them to the respective Congresses; Establish relationships with private entities in each of the member states, as well as international agencies and bureaus so as to obtain information and specialized assistance with matters of interest: Establish relationships targeting cooperation with Congresses of the nonmember nations and entities involved in regional integration schemes; Subscribe to cooperation and technical assistance accords with public and/or private entities whether domestic, <a href="/wiki/Supranational_union" title="Supranational union">supranational</a> or international. The Committee will be composed of a maximum of 64 acting parliamentary members, 16 per member state, and an equal number of alternates, appointed by the Congress to which they pertain, and with a term of office of at least two years. The meetings shall be conducted by a directors' board consisting of four presidents (one for each member state). The Committee will ordinarily meet twice a year, and extraordinarily whenever summoned by any of its five presidents. Meetings are held in the territory of each member state on a successive and alternating basis. Decision Making: Meetings of the Joint Parliamentary Committee will only be valid when attended by parliamentary delegations from all member states. Decisions by the Joint Parliamentary Committee will be made by consensus vote of the majority of the members accredited by the respective Congresses of each member state. Portuguese and Spanish are the official languages of the Joint Parliamentary Committee.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Trade_Commission">Trade Commission</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Trade Commission">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg/220px-Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="117" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg/330px-Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg/440px-Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3612" data-file-height="1918" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Stock_Exchange" class="mw-redirect" title="São Paulo Stock Exchange">São Paulo Stock Exchange</a>, the largest of <a href="/wiki/Latin_America" title="Latin America">Latin America</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>The Trade Commission will assist the Mercosur executive body, always striving to apply the instruments of <a href="/wiki/Common_trade_policy" class="mw-redirect" title="Common trade policy">common trade policy</a> agreed to by the member states for operation of the customs unification. The commission should also follow up on the development of issues and matters related to common trade policies, the intra-Mercosur trade and trade with other countries. The Commission will have five actual members and four alternates, with each member nation's indicating a member. The Trade Commission shall exert every effort to apply common trade policy instruments such as: trade agreements with other countries or international entities; administrative/commercial product lists; final adaptation system for Mercosur customs unification; rrigin system; <a href="/wiki/Free-trade_zone" title="Free-trade zone">free-trade zone</a> system, special customs areas and export processing zones; system to discourage unfair trade practices; elimination and harmonization of tariff restrictions; nonmember country safeguard systems; customs coordination and harmonization; <a href="/wiki/Consumer_protection" title="Consumer protection">consumer protection</a> systems; and export incentive harmonization.
</p><p>Furthermore, the trade commission should speak out regarding the issues raised by the member states regarding application and compliance with common offshore tariffs and other common trade policy instruments. The commission shall meet at least once a month, as well as whenever asked to by the Mercosur executive agency or by a member state. The commission can take decisions entailing administration and application of trade policies adopted under Southern Common Market, and whenever necessary submit proposals to the executive body regarding regulation of the areas under its authority; additionally, it can propose new guidelines or modify those in existence in Mercosur trade and customs matters. In this respect, the trade commission can propose a change in the import duty on specific items under <a href="/wiki/Common_external_tariff" title="Common external tariff">common external tariffs</a>, including cases referring to development of new Mercosur production activities. To better achieve its objectives, the trade commission can create technical committees targeting direction and supervision of the work it engages in. It can also adopt internal operating regulations. Proposals and decisions of the trade commission will be taken by a consensus of the representatives indicated by each member nation. Any disputes ensuing from the application, interpretation or compliance with the acts issued by the trade commission are referred to the Mercosur executive body, and should be resolved using the directives set forth in the <a href="/wiki/Dispute_Resolution" class="mw-redirect" title="Dispute Resolution">Dispute Resolution</a> System adopted under Southern Common Market.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_jurisdiction_over_contractual_matters">International jurisdiction over contractual matters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: International jurisdiction over contractual matters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="box-Unreferenced plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>does not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">cite</a> any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">sources</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit">improve this section</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">removed</a>.</span>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">July 2017</span>)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG/220px-Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG/330px-Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG/440px-Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG 2x" data-file-width="801" data-file-height="599" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Court of Mercosur, in the city of <a href="/wiki/Asunci%C3%B3n" title="Asunción">Asunción</a>, Paraguay</div></div></div>
<p>The rules on litigation jurisdiction over contractual matters will apply to disputes arising from <a href="/wiki/Civil_law_(common_law)" title="Civil law (common law)">civil</a> or commercial international contracts between private-law legal entities or individuals provided that: They are domiciled or headquartered in different member states: At least one of the parties to the contract is domiciled or headquartered in any member state and, additionally, has made a choice of jurisdiction in favor of a court in one of the member states. In this case, there must be a reasonable connection between the jurisdiction chosen and the controversy. The scope of the application of the international jurisdiction guidelines over contractual matters excludes the following: legal relationships between bankrupt entities/individuals and their creditors and any other analogous proceedings (especially concordatas composition with creditors); matters under agreements involving family and <a href="/wiki/Succession_law" class="mw-redirect" title="Succession law">succession law</a>; social security contracts; administrative contracts; employment contracts; consumer sales contracts; transport contracts; insurance policies; and rights in rem.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Choice_of_jurisdiction">Choice of jurisdiction</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Choice of jurisdiction">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Courts in member nations to whose jurisdiction the contracted parties have agreed to submit the matter in writing will have jurisdiction to settle controversies stemming from civil or commercial international contracts.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Agreement_of_choice">Agreement of choice</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Agreement of choice">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sat%C3%A9lites_SABIA-Mar_1_y_SABIA-Mar_2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Sat%C3%A9lites_SABIA-Mar_1_y_SABIA-Mar_2.jpg/220px-Sat%C3%A9lites_SABIA-Mar_1_y_SABIA-Mar_2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="79" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Sat%C3%A9lites_SABIA-Mar_1_y_SABIA-Mar_2.jpg/330px-Sat%C3%A9lites_SABIA-Mar_1_y_SABIA-Mar_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Sat%C3%A9lites_SABIA-Mar_1_y_SABIA-Mar_2.jpg/440px-Sat%C3%A9lites_SABIA-Mar_1_y_SABIA-Mar_2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2426" data-file-height="876" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sat%C3%A9lites_SABIA-Mar_1_y_SABIA-Mar_2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/SABIA-Mar" title="SABIA-Mar">SABIA-Mar</a>, scheduled to launch in 2022, is a <b>Brazilian/Argentine</b> earth observation satellite.</div></div></div>
<p>The jurisdiction can be agreed on at the time the contract is signed, during the life of the contract, or even when the dispute actually arises. The validity and effects of the choice of venue will be governed by the law of the member nations that normally have jurisdiction to hear the case, always resorting to the law most favorable to the validity of the contract. Whether or not jurisdiction is chosen, such jurisdiction will be prorogated in favor of the courts of the member state where the proceedings are in fact filed, provided the respondent voluntarily allows this in an affirmative and unfeigned way.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Subsidiary_jurisdiction">Subsidiary jurisdiction</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Subsidiary jurisdiction">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:13557727_894310980694612_437275486302448628_n_-_copia.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/13557727_894310980694612_437275486302448628_n_-_copia.jpg/220px-13557727_894310980694612_437275486302448628_n_-_copia.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/13557727_894310980694612_437275486302448628_n_-_copia.jpg/330px-13557727_894310980694612_437275486302448628_n_-_copia.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/13557727_894310980694612_437275486302448628_n_-_copia.jpg/440px-13557727_894310980694612_437275486302448628_n_-_copia.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="534" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:13557727_894310980694612_437275486302448628_n_-_copia.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mercosur Permanent Tribunal of Revision</div></div></div>
<p>Should the contracted parties not agree on courts competent to settle disputes, the member state chosen by the plaintiff of the case has jurisdiction—the court of the place where the contract is to be performed, the court of the domicile of the respondent, or the court of the <a href="/wiki/Domicile_(law)" title="Domicile (law)">domicile</a>, or headquarters of the claimant when the latter can show that it has done its part. For purposes of item (i) above the place of performance of the contract is the member state where the obligations on which the claim is based have been or should be performed, taking into consideration the following: For contracts involving certain specific items, the place where they existed at the time of contract signing; For contracts involving specific items according to their type, the place of domicile of the debtor at the time of contract signing; For contracts involving <a href="/wiki/Fungible" class="mw-redirect" title="Fungible">fungible</a> items, the place of domicile of the debtor at the time of conclusion of the contract; and For service rendering contracts:
</p>
<ul><li>If in regard to items, this the place where they were at the time of contract signing.</li>
<li>If effectiveness is related to any special place, this is the place where they were to produce effects.</li>
<li>In all other cases, this is the place of domicile of the debtor at the time of contract signing. For purposes of application of second item above for determination of the domicile of the respondent in a contractual dispute involving individuals, the following will be taken into consideration: The habitual residence: On a subsidiary basis, the central place of business; and In the absence of any such considerations, the place where found, meaning the actual residence. When dealing with a legal entity, the determination of the domicile will be based on where the administrative headquarters have been set up. The claim plaintiff can, as an alternative, file in any of the places where the legal entity has branches, establishments, agencies or any other type of representation. Legal entities headquartered in any member state that have concluded contracts with any other member state can be sued in the courts of this latter state should there be any dispute as to the construction and implementation of the obligations regulated by contract. In the event there is a codefendant, a suit on contractual matters can be adjudicated with the courts of jurisdiction in the territory of the domicile of any of the parties to the litigation. Additionally, any claims entailing personal <a href="/wiki/Collateral_contract" title="Collateral contract">collateral</a> rights or intervention of nonmember states in contractual obligations can be filed with the court hearing the main proceeding.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Counterclaims">Counterclaims</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Counterclaims">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the event of there being a counterclaim based on any act or fact that served as the basis for the main proceeding, the courts hearing the main proceeding will be competent to hear any counterclaims that may arise.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Educational_integration">Educational integration</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Educational integration">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="box-Unreferenced plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>does not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">cite</a> any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">sources</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit">improve this section</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">removed</a>.</span>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">July 2017</span>)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_(USP).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_%28USP%29.jpg/220px-Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_%28USP%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_%28USP%29.jpg/330px-Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_%28USP%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_%28USP%29.jpg/440px-Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_%28USP%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1717" data-file-height="1148" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_(USP).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/University_of_S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="University of São Paulo">University of São Paulo</a>, in <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="São Paulo">São Paulo</a>, Brazil, is one of the most highly esteemed university institutions in the region of Mercosur.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup></div></div></div>
<p>Based on the premise that education is a fundamental factor in the regional <a href="/wiki/Regional_integration" title="Regional integration">integration</a> process, educational courses at the primary or junior high level, provided that they do not entail technical studies, will be recognized by member states as being on the same level for all member nations. Likewise, to facilitate continuing education, course certificates issued by an institution accredited in one of the member states is valid in all other member states. Nontechnical primary and junior high level studies that have not been completed are accredited by any member state, thereby allowing course conclusion in another member nation. Studies are completed using an equivalency table to determine the level achieved.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Regional_technical_commission">Regional technical commission</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Regional technical commission">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>A regional technical commission harmonizes mechanisms for accreditation across member nations, and resolves any situation not be covered by the equivalency table. This commission includes delegations from the ministries of education of each member nation, and meets whenever at least two member states think it necessary. Meeting sites are established on a rotating basis. Any disputes among member states as a result of application, construction, or noncompliance regarding provisions related to education are initially resolved by direct diplomatic negotiations. Should the countries not reach an accord or only partially resolve the dispute, they resort to procedures set out in the <a href="/wiki/Dispute_resolution" title="Dispute resolution">dispute resolution</a> system. Should the member nations enter into a bilateral convention or accord with provisions more favorable to their students, the member states in question can apply whichever provisions they consider most advantageous.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Free_trade_zones">Free trade zones</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Free trade zones">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="box-More_citations_needed plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Refimprove" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>needs additional citations for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">verification</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit">improve this article</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and removed.<br /><small><span class="plainlinks"><i>Find sources:</i>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//www.google.com/search?as_eq=wikipedia&amp;q=%22Mercosur%22">"Mercosur"</a>&#160;–&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//www.google.com/search?tbm=nws&amp;q=%22Mercosur%22+-wikipedia">news</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//www.google.com/search?&amp;q=%22Mercosur%22+site:news.google.com/newspapers&amp;source=newspapers">newspapers</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//www.google.com/search?tbs=bks:1&amp;q=%22Mercosur%22+-wikipedia">books</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//scholar.google.com/scholar?q=%22Mercosur%22">scholar</a>&#160;<b>·</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.jstor.org/action/doBasicSearch?Query=%22Mercosur%22&amp;acc=on&amp;wc=on">JSTOR</a></span></small></span>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">July 2017</span>)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ushuaia_2009.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Ushuaia_2009.jpg/220px-Ushuaia_2009.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Ushuaia_2009.jpg/330px-Ushuaia_2009.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Ushuaia_2009.jpg/440px-Ushuaia_2009.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1280" data-file-height="960" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ushuaia_2009.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The Province of <a href="/wiki/Tierra_del_Fuego_Province_(Argentina)" class="mw-redirect" title="Tierra del Fuego Province (Argentina)">Tierra del Fuego</a> in Argentina has a free-trade zone.</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Teatro_Amazonas_-_Vista_A%C3%A9rea.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/Teatro_Amazonas_-_Vista_A%C3%A9rea.jpg/220px-Teatro_Amazonas_-_Vista_A%C3%A9rea.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/Teatro_Amazonas_-_Vista_A%C3%A9rea.jpg/330px-Teatro_Amazonas_-_Vista_A%C3%A9rea.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/Teatro_Amazonas_-_Vista_A%C3%A9rea.jpg/440px-Teatro_Amazonas_-_Vista_A%C3%A9rea.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4000" data-file-height="2667" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Teatro_Amazonas_-_Vista_A%C3%A9rea.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The city of <a href="/wiki/Manaus" title="Manaus">Manaus</a>, Brazil, has a free-trade zone.</div></div></div>
<p>The member nations can have commercial free-trade zones, industrial free-trade zones, export processing zones, and special customs areas, all of which target providing merchandise marketed or produced in these areas with treatment different from that afforded in their respective customs territories.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2013)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Uruguay's Vice-President <a href="/wiki/Danilo_Astori" title="Danilo Astori">Danilo Astori</a> said the issue of a free trade agreement with the United States must be dealt and that "opportunities must be built".  He also said that "each Mercosur country should have a multiplicity of memberships. Mercosur must have joint international policies, an agreement on moderate protection from third parties and above all must have agreements with other trade blocks".<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tariffs">Tariffs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Tariffs">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The member states can assess merchandise from these areas with the common external tariff used for Mercosur merchandise, or, in the case of certain special products, the domestic tariff prevailing in each individual state. In this way, the products from the free-trade zones can have the more favorable tax treatment established under Southern Common Market, given to the merchandise produced in the normal customs zones of each member state or, in the case of certain special products, can have the normal customs treatment prevailing in each nation. Products coming from outside of Mercosur are highly taxed so that local companies do not feel the need to compete with large international companies.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Safeguards">Safeguards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Safeguards">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Products produced or marketed in the <a href="/wiki/Free-trade_zone" title="Free-trade zone">free-trade zones</a> of each member nation will be eligible for the safeguard system whenever this entails an increase not provided for in imports, but capable of causing damages or threatened damages to the importer country.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Incentives">Incentives</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Incentives">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the event of the producing nation's granting special incentives for production from the free-trade zones that are not compatible with the corresponding guidelines established under the <a href="/wiki/General_Agreement_on_Tariffs_and_Trade" title="General Agreement on Tariffs and Trade">General Agreement on Tariffs and Trade</a> (GATT), the member nation can make any adjustments needed to return the situation to equilibrium.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Creation">Creation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Creation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The member nations agreed that any free-trade zones that in August 1994 were already in operation could operate normally under Mercosur, along with any that are set up in light of legal guidelines prevailing or in course in congress during this same time period. This means that a member nation can no longer create new free-trade zones that are more privileged.
Mercosur is an effective agreement for its members.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Manaus_and_Tierra_del_Fuego_FTZs">Manaus and Tierra del Fuego FTZs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Manaus and Tierra del Fuego FTZs">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The actual implementation of Mercosur will not affect the special <a href="/wiki/Manaus" title="Manaus">Manaus</a>, Brazil, and <a href="/wiki/Tierra_del_Fuego_Province,_Argentina" title="Tierra del Fuego Province, Argentina">Tierra del Fuego</a>, Argentina, free-trade zones organized in light of their special geographic situations. These two free-trade zones may continue normal operations until 2013.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Reciprocal_promotion_and_protection">Reciprocal promotion and protection</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Reciprocal promotion and protection">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="box-Unreferenced plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>does not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">cite</a> any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">sources</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit">improve this section</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">removed</a>.</span>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">July 2017</span>)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:CUPULAMERCOSUL.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/CUPULAMERCOSUL.jpg/220px-CUPULAMERCOSUL.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="335" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/CUPULAMERCOSUL.jpg/330px-CUPULAMERCOSUL.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/a/a4/CUPULAMERCOSUL.jpg 2x" data-file-width="353" data-file-height="538" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:CUPULAMERCOSUL.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Celso_Amorim" title="Celso Amorim">Celso Amorim</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luiz_In%C3%A1cio_Lula_da_Silva" title="Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva">Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva</a>, <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A9rgio_Cabral" class="mw-redirect" title="Sérgio Cabral">Sérgio Cabral</a> during the leadership of Mercosur/Mercosul.</div></div></div>
<p>The nations subscribing to the <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Asunci%C3%B3n" title="Treaty of Asunción">Asunción Treaty</a> consider that the creation and maintenance of conditions favorable to individual or corporate investment for the jurisdiction of one of the member states in the territory of another state is essential to intensify the economic cooperation targeted so as to accelerate the integration process among all four member states. In this context, Argentina, Uruguay, Paraguay and Brazil signed on 1 January 1994 in the city of <a href="/wiki/Colonia_del_Sacramento" title="Colonia del Sacramento">Colonia del Sacramento</a>, Uruguay, the Colonia Protocol for the Reciprocal Promotion and Protection of Mercosur Investments (Colonia Protocol). It was established in this protocol that investments under Mercosur by investors resident or domiciled in the territory of any member state will be entitled to treatment no less favorable than that accorded by the other member state to national investors or nonmember states.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Investors">Investors</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Investors">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>For the purposes of constructing the <a href="/wiki/Colonia_(United_States)" title="Colonia (United States)">Colonia</a> Protocol, investors are considered to be: Individuals who are citizens of any of the member nations or that reside there on a permanent basis or are domiciled there, with due regard for legislation prevailing in such territory; Legal entities organized pursuant to the legislation of one of the member nations that are headquartered there; and Legal entities organized in the territory where the investment is made, actually and directly or indirectly controlled by the legal entities or individuals mentioned above.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Investment">Investment</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Investment">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The term investment includes all types of assets such as: movable or immovable property, such as rights in rem and guarantee in rem rights; shares, corporate holdings and any other type of corporate participation; credit instruments and rights that may have an economic value; intellectual property rights or materials, Including copyrights and <a href="/wiki/Industrial_property" title="Industrial property">industrial property</a> rights such as patents, industrial drawings, trademarks, commercial names, technical procedures, know-how and goodwill; Economic concessions involving <a href="/wiki/Public_law" title="Public law">public law</a>, such as research, cultivation, extraction or natural resource exploration concessions.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Freedom_to_invest">Freedom to invest</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Freedom to invest">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ponte_Internacional_Bar%C3%A3o_de_Mau%C3%A1_como_Patrim%C3%B4nio_Cultural_do_MERCOSUL_na_cidade_de_Jaguar%C3%A3o_(18125301660).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Ponte_Internacional_Bar%C3%A3o_de_Mau%C3%A1_como_Patrim%C3%B4nio_Cultural_do_MERCOSUL_na_cidade_de_Jaguar%C3%A3o_%2818125301660%29.jpg/220px-Ponte_Internacional_Bar%C3%A3o_de_Mau%C3%A1_como_Patrim%C3%B4nio_Cultural_do_MERCOSUL_na_cidade_de_Jaguar%C3%A3o_%2818125301660%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Ponte_Internacional_Bar%C3%A3o_de_Mau%C3%A1_como_Patrim%C3%B4nio_Cultural_do_MERCOSUL_na_cidade_de_Jaguar%C3%A3o_%2818125301660%29.jpg/330px-Ponte_Internacional_Bar%C3%A3o_de_Mau%C3%A1_como_Patrim%C3%B4nio_Cultural_do_MERCOSUL_na_cidade_de_Jaguar%C3%A3o_%2818125301660%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Ponte_Internacional_Bar%C3%A3o_de_Mau%C3%A1_como_Patrim%C3%B4nio_Cultural_do_MERCOSUL_na_cidade_de_Jaguar%C3%A3o_%2818125301660%29.jpg/440px-Ponte_Internacional_Bar%C3%A3o_de_Mau%C3%A1_como_Patrim%C3%B4nio_Cultural_do_MERCOSUL_na_cidade_de_Jaguar%C3%A3o_%2818125301660%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2821" data-file-height="1881" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ponte_Internacional_Bar%C3%A3o_de_Mau%C3%A1_como_Patrim%C3%B4nio_Cultural_do_MERCOSUL_na_cidade_de_Jaguar%C3%A3o_(18125301660).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Brazil–Uruguay international border</div></div></div>
<p>The nation receiving the investment cannot avail itself of unjustified or discriminatory means capable of restricting the investor's freedom to manage, maintain, use, enjoy and dispose of its investments.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tax">Tax</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Tax">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The member states are not however obligated to extend to investors in the other nations signatory to the Colonia Protocol the <a href="/wiki/Cost%E2%80%93benefit_analysis" title="Cost–benefit analysis">benefits</a> of any treatment, preference or <a href="/wiki/Privilege_(legal_ethics)" class="mw-redirect" title="Privilege (legal ethics)">privilege</a> resulting from international accords relating fully or partially to tax matters.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Exceptions">Exceptions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Exceptions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In addition, the member nations can temporarily establish a list of exceptions where the new treatment will not yet prevail.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg/220px-Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg/330px-Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg/440px-Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1600" data-file-height="1200" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Landmark of the Three Borders – Argentina, Brazil, and Paraguay, in <a href="/wiki/Foz_do_Igua%C3%A7u" title="Foz do Iguaçu">Foz do Iguaçu</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>In this way, the various member nations decided to except the following economic sectors:
</p>
<ul><li><b>Argentina:</b> ownership of real estate on the frontier strip, air transportation, naval industry, nuclear power plants, uranium mining, insurance and fishery;</li>
<li><b>Brazil:</b> mineral prospecting and mining; use of <a href="/wiki/Hydraulic_energy" class="mw-redirect" title="Hydraulic energy">hydraulic energy</a>; health care; television and radio broadcasting and telecommunications in general, acquisition or leasing of rural properties; participation in the financial <a href="/wiki/Intermediation" title="Intermediation">intermediation</a>, insurance, social security and capitalization systems; chartering and cabotage as well as inland navigation;</li>
<li><b>Paraguay:</b> ownership of real property on the frontier strip; communications, including radio and television broadcasting; air, sea and land transportation; electricity, water and telephone services; prospecting for hydrocarbons and strategic minerals; import and refining of petroleum derivatives and postal services;</li>
<li><b>Uruguay:</b> electricity; hydrocarbons; basic petrochemicals, atomic energy; prospecting for strategic minerals; financial intermediation; railways, telecommunications; radio broadcasting; press and audiovisual means.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Expropriation_and_compensation">Expropriation and compensation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Expropriation and compensation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The member nations undertook to do nothing to <a href="/wiki/Nationalize" class="mw-redirect" title="Nationalize">nationalize</a> or expropriate investments in their territories that pertain to investors from the signatory countries, unless such measures are taken based on public need. In such case, nothing discriminatory can be done, but everything must be implemented by due legal process. Compensation for the investment holder that is expropriated or nationalized should be both adequate and effective, and made in advance, based on the real investment value determined at the time the decision is publicly announced by the proper authorities. This payment will be updated until actual payment, and the affected investor will receive interest.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Transfers">Transfers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Transfers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The original member state investors will be ensured free transfer of their investments and any earnings thereon. These transfers can be made in freely convertible currency, using the <a href="/wiki/Exchange_rate" title="Exchange rate">exchange rate</a> prevailing on the market pursuant to the procedures established by the member state receiving the investment. Member nations cannot adopt any exchange measures restricting free transfer of the funds invested or from activities exercised in their respective territories.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Role_and_potential">Role and potential</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Role and potential">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg/220px-Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="119" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg/330px-Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg/440px-Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2500" data-file-height="1357" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Plenary Session of the 49th Mercosur Summit in <a href="/wiki/Asunci%C3%B3n" title="Asunción">Asuncion</a>, December 28, 2015.</div></div></div>
<p>Some South Americans see Mercosur as giving the capability to combine resources to balance the activities of other global economic powers, especially the <a href="/wiki/North_American_Free_Trade_Agreement" title="North American Free Trade Agreement">North American Free Trade Agreement</a> (NAFTA) and the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> The organization could also potentially pre-empt the <a href="/wiki/Free_Trade_Area_of_the_Americas" title="Free Trade Area of the Americas">Free Trade Area of the Americas</a> (FTAA);<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> however, over half of the current Mercosur member countries rejected the FTAA proposal at the IV Cumbre de las Américas (<a href="/wiki/4th_Summit_of_the_Americas" title="4th Summit of the Americas">IV Summit of the Americas</a>) in Argentina in 2005.
</p><p>The development of Mercosur was arguably weakened by <a href="/wiki/1998%E2%80%932002_Argentine_great_depression" title="1998–2002 Argentine great depression">the collapse of the Argentine economy in 2001</a> and it has still seen internal conflicts over trade policy, between Brazil and Argentina, Argentina and Uruguay, Paraguay and Brazil, etc. In addition, many obstacles must be addressed before the development of a common currency in Mercosur.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2004, Mercosur signed a cooperation agreement with the <a href="/wiki/Andean_Community_of_Nations" class="mw-redirect" title="Andean Community of Nations">Andean Community of Nations</a> trade bloc (CAN) and they published a joint letter of intent for future negotiations towards integrating all of South America.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> The prospect of increased political integration within the organization, as per the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> and advocated by some, is still uncertain.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Bolivia, also a member of CAN and an associate member of Mercosur before the UNASUR process started, plays a crucial part in relations, says Marion Hörmann, since Bolivia is traditionally seen as a mediator between the Andean countries and the rest of South America. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20110927084954/http://www.inwent.org/ez/articles/168821/index.en.shtml">Regional Integration: Key Role for Bolivia</a>
</p><p>The bloc comprises a population of more than <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_population" class="mw-redirect" title="List of countries by population">270 million people</a>, and the combined Gross Domestic Product of the full-member nations is in excess of US$3.0 trillion a year (<a href="/wiki/Purchasing_power_parity" title="Purchasing power parity">Purchasing power parity</a>, PPP) according to <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">International Monetary Fund</a> (IMF) numbers, making Mercosur the <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(PPP)" title="List of countries by GDP (PPP)">fifth-largest</a> economy in the World. It is the fourth-largest trading bloc after the European Union.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The working of Mercosur has not met with universal approval within interested countries. Chile has to a certain extent preferred to pursue bilateral agreements with trading partners, and there have been calls from Uruguayan politicians to follow this example.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="FTA_with_third_parties">FTA with third parties</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: FTA with third parties">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg/220px-Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="59" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg/330px-Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg/440px-Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3287" data-file-height="876" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Vehicle_registration_plates_of_the_Mercosur" title="Vehicle registration plates of the Mercosur">Mercosur common plates</a>, in use since January 2016</div></div></div>
<p>With the 2005 cooperation agreement with Mercosur, the <a href="/wiki/Andean_Community" title="Andean Community">Andean Community</a> gained four new associate members: Argentina, Brazil, Paraguay, and Uruguay. These four Mercosur members were granted associate membership by the Andean Council of Foreign Ministers meeting in an enlarged session with the Commission (of the Andean Community) on 7 July 2005. This move reciprocates the actions of Mercosur, which granted associate membership to all the Andean Community nations by virtue of the Economic Complementarity Agreements (<a href="/wiki/Free_Trade_Agreement" class="mw-redirect" title="Free Trade Agreement">Free Trade Agreements</a>) signed between the CAN and individual Mercosur members.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:FTAMercosurEU.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/FTAMercosurEU.jpg/220px-FTAMercosurEU.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="220" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/FTAMercosurEU.jpg/330px-FTAMercosurEU.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/FTAMercosurEU.jpg/440px-FTAMercosurEU.jpg 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="600" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:FTAMercosurEU.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Free trade agreement between EU and Mercosur</div></div></div>
<p>Mercosur signed free trade agreements with Israel in December 2007,<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> with Egypt in August 2010,<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/State_of_Palestine" title="State of Palestine">State of Palestine</a> in December 2011<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a> on December 18, 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2016, Brazilian presidents, <a href="/wiki/Dilma_Rousseff" title="Dilma Rousseff">Dilma Rousseff</a> and later <a href="/wiki/Michel_Temer" title="Michel Temer">Michel Temer</a>, along with Argentine President <a href="/wiki/Mauricio_Macri" title="Mauricio Macri">Macri</a> began to place pressure to negotiate a <a href="/wiki/Free-trade_area" title="Free-trade area">free trade agreement</a> between Mercosur and the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> and other Latin American nations.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> In June 2019, the <a href="/wiki/European_Union%E2%80%93Mercosur_Free_Trade_Agreement" class="mw-redirect" title="European Union–Mercosur Free Trade Agreement">European Union–Mercosur Free Trade Agreement</a> was confirmed.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> The bilateral trade deal opens 100 percent of EU trade and 90 percent of Mercosur trade. <sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> The deal still needs to be ratified, however.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Suspended_members">Suspended members</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Suspended members">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Observer_countries">Observer countries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Observer countries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<li><a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a></li></ul>
<p><a href="/wiki/Guyana" title="Guyana">Guyana</a> and <a href="/wiki/Suriname" title="Suriname">Suriname</a> have signed a framework agreement with Mercosur in July 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> However, this proposal requires legislative approval.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: See also">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
